<div class="document"><br><h1><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">K8S网络模型介绍</span><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h1>

<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">基本要求</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<ul style="list-style-type:disc;"><li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-0pt pap-spacing-after-4pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:100%;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:5.333333333333333px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#222222;background:#ffffff;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">节点上的 Pod 可以不通过 NAT 和所有 Pod 通信</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
</ul><ul style="list-style-type:disc;"><li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-0pt pap-spacing-after-4pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:100%;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:5.333333333333333px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#222222;background:#ffffff;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">节点上的代理（比如：kubelet） 可以和本节点上的所有Pod通信</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
</ul><ul style="list-style-type:disc;"><li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-0pt pap-spacing-after-4pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:100%;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:5.333333333333333px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#222222;background:#ffffff;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">HostNetwork 类型的 Pod 可以不通过 NAT 和所有 Pod 通信（仅针对支持 HostNetwork Pod 的平台：Linux）</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
</ul><p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">网络模型定义K8S网络规范，K8S Service和NetworkPolicy这些概念构建在该模型之上。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">该模型下每个Pod都可以被视为虚拟机/物理机。Pod中的容器可以被视为虚拟机/物理机中的进程，便于应用从虚拟机/物理机迁移到Pod。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h1><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">社区网络方案介绍</span><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h1>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">额外封包</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">Flannel-VXLAN/Calico-IPIP</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">控制面介绍</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">一个节点关联一个PodCIDR，容器网络和节点网络分属两个网络平面</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">数据面介绍</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">Host1:PodCidr 10.10.1.0/24</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">Host2:PodCidr 10.10.2.0/24</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">Host1容器A访问Host2容器A，数据包从容器A发出，达到br0，进行路由查找，命中相应规则，转发到vtep0，vtep0是一个vxlan设备，先进行内层vxlan报文封装，依据下一跳找到mac地址，完成内层vxlan报文封装，接着依据下一跳mac地址从fdb表项找到可路由的外层目的IP，完成外层vxlan报文封装，最终由eth0发出，路由到Host2，Host2收包，解封vxlan，转发到容器A，回包类似。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1280px; height: 572.8px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(2)" width="1200" height="572" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; height: 572.8px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">为什么TKE没有采用该方案</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<ul style="list-style-type:disc;"><li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#FF0000;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">该方案可以跑在云上，不过性能损失严重（</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">吞吐方面，全局路由要比VxLAN高40%，时延要小5%~10%），具体可以参考 @zhiguohong 文章 </span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">https://cloud.tencent.com/developer/article/1006675</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#FF0000;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">因为额外封装，网络问题定位较困难，比较难trace</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
</ul><h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">直接路由</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">Calico-BGP</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">控制面介绍</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">一个节点关联一个PodCIDR，容器网络和节点网络在同一个网络平面</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">数据面介绍</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 593px; height: 305px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(3)" width="593" height="305" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; width: 593px; height: 305px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt=""></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">每一个节点都会有一个BGP client进行BGP路由的维护，跨节点Pod互访，数据包从节点发出，到达交换机后，由交换机转发相应的节点完成网络链路访问</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">为什么TKE没有采用该方案</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">利用BGP来联通容器网络，需要节点上层交换机感知容器路由，并支持BGP协议，VPC不支持该方案（黑石1.0除外）</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h1><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">TKE网络方案介绍</span><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h1>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">基于性能考虑，TKE采用了直接路由方案，节点间数据包的路由由VPC保证，节点内会配置网桥/策略路由实现数据包能正确发送给容器或让容器发出的数据包由节点正确的网卡发出。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">全局路由</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">背景</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<ol start="1" style="list-style-type:decimal;"><li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">基于社区控制面方案，简单可靠</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">Pod销毁重建比较频繁，Pod底层网络配置好之后，节点内Pod网络配置可以在节点内闭环，保证Pod快速启动/销毁</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">一个节点固定关联一个容器小网段，用户不需要也不应该关心容器使用的IP，符合云原生理念</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
</ol><p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1280px; height: 334.2px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(4)" width="1200" height="334" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; height: 334.2px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">数据面</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">互通</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1232px; height: 674px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(5)" width="1200" height="674" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; height: 674px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">数据包从Pod1发出，到达cbr0，走默认路由转发到eth0，VPC母鸡根据全局路由表项，转发到Node2，eth0收包，查找路由转发到cbr0，经过网桥二层转发到Pod2，回包类似。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">访问外网</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1048px; height: 493px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(6)" width="1048" height="493" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; width: 1048px; height: 493px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">具体可以参考文章 </span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">http://km.oa.com/group/31235/articles/show/396937</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">控制面</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">节点网段分配管理</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 428px; height: 217px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(7)" width="428" height="217" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; width: 428px; height: 217px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt=""></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1280px; height: 435.667px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(8)" width="1200" height="435" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; height: 435.667px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">具体可以参考文章 </span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">http://km.oa.com/group/31235/articles/show/395393</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">Pod IP的分配管理</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">依赖于 CNI host-local 插件</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">共享网卡</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">背景</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<ol start="1" style="list-style-type:decimal;"><li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">在容器化的进程中，有些用户的业务系统（配置管理，监控，鉴权）强依赖于IP，改造成本高，需要实现Pod重建后可以固定IP（全局路由方案一个节点上的容器IP是固定的，无法实现Pod迁移后IP不变）</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">全局路由方案容器网段位于VPC CIDR之外，不能直接使用云上资源（CLB，NAT，EIP等），只能依赖于节点做中转。为了实现全局路由方案跨地域，跨IDC容器的互访需要各云网关额外适配，支持成本高，为此需要实现Pod直接使用VPC内IP。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
</ol><p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1280px; height: 997.267px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(9)" width="1200" height="997" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; height: 997.267px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#FF0000;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">数据面</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">互通</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1280px; height: 723.867px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(10)" width="1200" height="723" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; height: 723.867px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">数据包从Pod1发出，到达veth0，查找策略路由table 1，经由eth1发出，VPC母机将数据包转发到Node2，eth1收包，查找策略路由转发到veth0，交由Pod2，回包类似。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">访问外网</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">同全局路由，不过因为策略路由方案Pod使用的VPC IP，故可以支持使用 NAT，EIP</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">控制面</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">集群侧组件</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1280px; height: 724.867px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(11)" width="1200" height="724" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; height: 724.867px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">中控组件 ipamd 负责监听节点的增加/删除事件，进行弹性网卡的创建和IP分配，并将弹性网卡和IP信息存储到CRD-NodeENIConfig中。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">节点侧组件</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1280px; height: 610.733px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(12)" width="1200" height="610" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; height: 610.733px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">eni-agent会监听CRD-NodeENIConfig的创建/更新事件，同步节点内IPAM信息，Pod创建时，kubelet会调用CNI，然后通过 GRPC 请求到 eni-agent，eni-agent负责节点内Pod IPAM，tke-route-eni 负责节点和容器网络协议栈的配置。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">具体可参考 </span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">https://git.code.oa.com/tke/eni-cni-static-ipamd</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">方案对比</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
