<h1><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">K8S负载均衡介绍</span><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h1>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">负载均衡要解决的问题</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">虽然每个Pod都有一个独立的IP，但是为了实现业务可以水平扩展，大多数服务都会支持多副本。另外Pod的生命周期比较短，一个服务中Pod IP列表是不断变化的，所以服务访问的时候使用Pod IP是不现实的。为此K8S引入了Service来实现了多副本的统一接入和负载均衡。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1280px; height: 319.067px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(13)" width="1200" height="319" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; height: 319.067px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">Service概念介绍</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1280px; height: 729.667px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(14)" width="1200" height="729" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; height: 729.667px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">service是一个抽象的概念，是K8S用于实现一组Pod作为网络服务的抽象访问，一组Pod的集合通常是用标签选择出来的，service在形式上暴露为一个虚拟的IP，kube-proxy利用iptables/IPVS实现针对该虚拟IP的访问会负载均衡到该组Pod集合。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">service类别</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">ClusterIP：集群内负载均衡</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">NodePort：基于节点端口实现的集群外负载均衡</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">LoadBalancer：基于外部负载均衡器实现的集群外负载均衡</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">ClusterIP Service介绍</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">集群内负载均衡，基于iptables DNAT规则实现service负载均衡到后端Pod</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1280px; height: 362px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(15)" width="1200" height="362" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; height: 362px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">NodePort Service介绍</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">基于节点端口实现的集群外负载均衡，是LoadBalancer Service的实现基础，除了做DNAT，还会做SNAT</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1280px; height: 401px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(16)" width="1200" height="401" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; height: 401px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">LoadBalancer Service介绍</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">基于外部负载均衡器和NodePort实现的集群外负载均衡，需要走两套负载均衡的逻辑</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1280px; height: 310.667px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(17)" width="1200" height="310" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; height: 310.667px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">TKE上负责LoadBalancer Service实现的组件---service-controller</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">tke-service-controller介绍</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">TKE自研的service控制器组件，监听service的增删改事件，对接CLB的接口，创建CLB并绑定到NodePort</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">LB直通Pod</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">不再经过NodePort，由LB直接转发给Pod，性能上更优；统一的负载均衡视图，不会因为二次负载均衡造成负载不均</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">IPV6支持（NAT64）</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">支持外网通过IPV6访问到后端服务</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">具体可参考 </span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">https://git.code.oa.com/k8s/service-controller/tree/master/test/cases</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">Kube-Proxy介绍</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">运行在节点上的网络代理，作为K8S Service的控制面组件，负责实现ClusterIP/NodePort Service到iptables/IPVS规则的映射</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">iptables</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">配置DNAT规则实现Service到后端服务的负载均衡</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">IPVS</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">利用内核模块IPVS实现负载均衡</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">iptables VS. IPVS</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">这里引用了外部结论，为了比较两种方案的性能差异，主要对比了RTT时延和CPU消耗</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">RTT时延</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 974px; height: 520px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(18)" width="974" height="520" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; width: 974px; height: 520px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<ul style="list-style-type:disc;"><li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">长链接情况下iptables/IPVS方案RTT时延没有明显差别</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">Service的数目超过1000后，短连接RTT时延的开始显现出差别</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
</ul><p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">对于iptables和IPVS来说，RTT时延的差别主要和新建连接有关，和请求的数目没有关系。因为一个数据包如果命中conntrack规则后，无需走iptables/IPVS规则。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">CPU消耗</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 974px; height: 518px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(19)" width="974" height="518" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; width: 974px; height: 518px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<ul style="list-style-type:disc;"><li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">Service的数目超过1000后，CPU消耗开始显现出差别</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">在Service的数目达到10000（100000个Pod）后，iptables单核CPU消耗在35%，IPVS在8%</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
</ul><h5><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">CPU消耗的具体原因</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h5>
<ol start="1" style="list-style-type:decimal;"><li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">默认情况下kube-proxy每隔30s进行iptables/IPVS规则的同步，老内核下iptables的同步会更消耗CPU</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">iptables模式下，新建连接需要O(N)的时间复杂度，而IPVS只需要O(1)的时间复杂度</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
</ol><h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">选择 iptables 还是 IPVS</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<ul style="list-style-type:disc;"><li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">当service数目在1000+，IPVS在性能上会更好。如果服务中大多是长链接，并且内核也较新，性能上的差异不会很大，但是如果服务中大多是短链接，并且内核也较老，可以选择IPVS模式</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">IPVS支持更多负载均衡策略，如果有这类需求，选择IPVS模式</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">如果不确定是否应该选择IPVS，可以继续使用iptables，因为它在生产中进行了更多的优化，并且是默认设置</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
</ul><h1><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">K8S服务发现介绍</span><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h1>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">服务发现要解决的问题</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">使用域名而不是IP实现服务的访问，可读性高，用户可以自定义访问服务名</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">服务注册</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:0pt;font-family:monospace, &#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, <p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">服务名由Service的名称和命名空间组成，DNS中控服务组件（KubeDNS/CoreDNS）List-Watch Service/Pod/Endpoint的变化将服务名和IP的对应关系同步到内存</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">服务发现</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 800px; height: 600px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(21)" width="601" height="451" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; width: 601px; height: 451px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">K8S基于DNS实现了服务发现，DNS中控服务组件以Service的形式暴露在集群，业务Pod使用DNS服务组件的Service作为NameServer，发起的DNS请求会经由Service负载均衡到中控服务组件，中控服务组件处理DNS请求。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">部署NodeLocalDNS组件后，NodeLocalDNS会作为缓存层，该节点上业务Pod发起的DNS会先经过NodeLocalDNS组件，如果命中缓存，直接返回给业务Pod。否则由NodeLocalDNS组件发起到中控服务组件的DNS请求。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">NodeLocalDNS解决的问题</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<ul style="list-style-type:disc;"><li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">使用节点级别的缓存，降低时延，减少中控DNS组件压力</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">跳过iptables DNAT和连接跟踪减少 conntrack竞争（</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/56903</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">）</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">从本地缓存代理到中控DNS组件的连接升级为TCP，降低因UDP丢包造成的延迟</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
</ul><h1><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">K8S NetworkPolicy介绍</span><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h1>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">以应用为中心的网络概念，允许用户指定Pod和其他网络实体（某些命名空间的Pod，IPBlock）的访问策略</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">功能举例</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 375px; height: 361px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(22)" width="375" height="361" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; width: 375px; height: 361px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt=""></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span
