SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">该 NetworkPolicy 作用于 default 命名空间下 label 包含 </span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;text-decoration:underline;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">app: test-service</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"> 的 Pod 集合，允许 default 命名空间下 label 包含 </span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;text-decoration:underline;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">app: client-green</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"> Pod 访问，拒绝其他访问。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">TKE支持的NetworkPolicy插件</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">calico，kube-router</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h1><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">TKE新一代网络方案介绍</span><span style="font-size:18pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h1>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">背景</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">随着容器技术的发展成熟，越来越多的组件迁移到容器，在技术迁移过程中，数据库，游戏，AI这些组件对容器网络性能（时延，吞吐，稳定性）提出了更高的要求。为了得到更优的时延和吞吐表现，各大云厂商都在致力于缩短节点内容器的网络访问链路，让数据包能尽可能快地转发到容器网卡。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">数据面</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">互通</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 1023px; height: 564px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(23)" width="1023" height="564" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; width: 1023px; height: 564px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">数据包从Pod 10.0.0.2发出，不再经过节点默认网络协议栈，由VPC母机将数据包转发 Pod 10.0.0.10，回包类似。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">访问外网</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">依赖于 NAT，EIP</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">性能表现</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#000000;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">基础网络性能</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#000000;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#000000;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">极大缩短了容器访问链路，缩短了访问时延，并使PPS 可以达到整机上限</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#000000;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h4><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#000000;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">业务网络性能</span><span style="font-size:12pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#000000;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h4>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#000000;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">为了得到不同网络方案下的QPS，这里控制变量，让不同网络方案的nginx Pod运行在同一节点，使用 wrk 分别压测不同Pod，并让服务端节点的 cpu 接近 100%</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 702px; height: 682px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(24)" width="702" height="682" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; width: 702px; height: 682px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt="" class="amplify"></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span class="image-wrapper" style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 638px; height: 686px;"><img src="./Kubernetes网络系统介绍 - Kubernetes - KM平台_files/cos-file-url(25)" width="638" height="686" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-top: 0px; width: 638px; height: 686px; position: relative; z-index: 2;" alt=""></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">控制面</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<h3><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">节点弹性网卡分配管理</span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h3>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">为了兼顾Pod启动速度并缓解对VPC弹性网卡接口的压力，实现了网卡池，可以将空闲的网卡维持在一定的水位</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">集群内负载均衡介绍</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">由于不再经过节点网络协议栈，传统基于 iptables 和 IPVS 的 ClusterIP service 访问方案不能直接适用于该方案。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">为了实现该方案下 Pod 可以直接访问 ClusterIP service，TKE实现了 share-NS IPVS 方案，使得在容器网络命名空间下也可以访问到节点网络协议栈的 IPVS 规则。</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">具体可参考 @jianmingfan 大佬PR https://git.code.oa.com/tlinux/tkernel4/merge_requests/29</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
<h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">其他功能介绍</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<ol start="1" style="list-style-type:decimal;"><li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">支持Pod绑定EIP/NAT，不再依赖节点的外网访问能力，无须做SNAT，可以满足直播、游戏、视频会议等高并发，高带宽外网</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#000000;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">访问场景</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">支持Pod绑定安全组，实现Pod级别的安全隔离</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">支持基于Pod名称的固定IP，Pod重新调度后仍能保证IP不变</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;padding-left:0em;">
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt pap-hanging-indent-1.6em" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">支持CLB直通Pod，不再经过NodePort转发，提升转发性能并拥有统一的负载均衡视图</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
</li>
</ol><h2><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">怎么创建独立网卡方案</span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#1A1A1A;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></h2>
<p class="paragraph text-align-type-left pap-line-1.3 pap-line-rule-auto pap-spacing-before-3pt pap-spacing-after-3pt" style="text-align:left;line-height:130%;margin-top:4px;margin-bottom:4px;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;">申请新一代容器网络方案内测开通后，创建TKE集群时选择VPC-CNI/Pod独立网卡模式即可</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, &#39;Helvetica Neue&#39;, Helvetica, &#39;PingFang SC&#39;, &#39;Microsoft YaHei&#39;, &#39;Source Han Sans SC&#39;, &#39;Noto Sans CJK SC&#39;, &#39;WenQuanYi Micro Hei&#39;, sans-serif;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;color:#333333;background:transparent;letter-spacing:0pt;vertical-align:baseline;"></span></p>
